defined_text = {
	name = GetStateName_1
	text = {
		trigger = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_1_FRA 	#Corse
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = SAD
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_1_SAD	#Còssiga
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GER
					original_tag = AUS
					original_tag = SWI
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_1_GER	#Korsika
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { #default name if none of the above is controller OR prohibited in game rules
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = r56_state_renaming_prohibited_flag
				controller = {
					NOT = {
						original_tag = FRA
						original_tag = SAD
						original_tag = GER
						original_tag = AUS
						original_tag = SWI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_1
	}
}

		trigger = {
			controller = {

					original_tag = FAK
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_908
	}

		trigger = { #default name if none of the above is controller OR prohibited in game rules

				has_global_flag = r56_state_renaming_prohibited_flag
				controller = {
					NOT = {
						original_tag = FAK
					}
				}
			}
		}
		localization_key = STATE_908
	}
